2/26/23, 9:01â€¯PM - Aditya Patil: from smelting furnace[I], we get slag and matte which needs to be separated in electric furnace[II]. The slag in II consist of higher copper content due to oxidation of Cu2S in I furnace to form Cu2O . Now, in order to remove this copper from slag and turn it into matte, we use coke and pyrite...â€¦.coke reduces Cu2O directly to form Copper metal which settles down in matte due to high density where it reacts with FeS to from Cu2S and become a part of matte...â€¦.also, pyrite hai formula FeS2, so probably FeS2 reacts with Cu2O to give FeO and Cu2S as copper has high affinity for S and Fe has high affinity for O...â€¦..in this way the copper content dropped(decopperization) due to addition of coke and pyrites in II furnace ğŸ™‚ğŸ™‚

2/28/23, 7:07â€¯PM - Sudarsan Ramakrishnan IITR Meta: In summary, collapsibility and friability are two different properties of foundry cores that relate to how the cores behave when they are exposed to different types of stresses. Collapsibility refers to how the core behaves when it is subjected to high temperatures and pressure, while friability refers to how the core behaves when it is handled or transported.

3/3/23, 4:40â€¯PM - Harshit Garg IITR Meta: Consumer theory me hamara assumption hh consumers are rational thinkers and so we assume the conditon of transitivity, means if A > B and B>C; implies A>C. So if we assume two curves with utility U1 and U2 (U2>U1) with A and B on U1 and C on U2 (A being point of intersection) than that would mean A=B and A=C , implies B=C, but since B and C lies on different curves, B != C. Implies our assumption is wrong and so two indifference curves can never intersect

3/4/23, 3:07â€¯AM - Harshit Garg IITR Meta: At very high temperatures, the movement of dislocations is primarily controlled by thermally-activated mechanisms, such as vacancy diffusion. This means that the mobility of dislocations is not significantly affected by the presence of solute atoms or other obstacles, and therefore, the formation of serrations is suppressed.

On the other hand, at very low temperatures, dislocation motion is primarily controlled by the Peierls-Nabarro mechanism, which involves the formation of kinks or jogged segments in the dislocation line. The motion of dislocations by this mechanism is less sensitive to the presence of solute atoms or other obstacles, which makes the formation of serrations less likely.

6/4/23, 11:44â€¯AM - Shreyansh Tiwari IITR Meta: Steps to Vote:
1. Go to election.iitr.ac.in
2. Click the blue button with the text "Vote"
3. if you are not logged in to channeli, you will be redirected to channeli login page, just enter your channeli credentials and hit login ( if you are already logged in, this page will not appear, just move to the next step )
4. It will ask you to allow the election portal to be able to access your channeli data ( we are using it to determine whom you will be able to vote ) just click allow
5. Select the candidates you want to vote for, in each position
6. Once selected candidates for each position, review that you have selected the candidate you want to vote for ( the selected candidates will be highlighted ) and also that there is no position with none of the candidates selected
7. Go to the bottom and click submit vote button
Note: You have to vote for each position, you will not be able to submit your vote (i.e submit button will not be active), when no candidate is chosen for one or more positions
